And across it all, we’ve embedded financial services tools at the point of sale, so merchants can access a business loan and manage their cash flow all in one place.&amp;lt;br&amp;gt;&amp;lt;br&amp;gt;Today, we’re a partner to sellers of all sizes – large, enterprise-scale businesses with complex commerce operations, sellers just starting out, as well as merchants who began selling with Square and have grown larger over time. As our sellers scale, so do our solutions. We all grow together.&amp;lt;br&amp;gt;&amp;lt;br&amp;gt;There is a massive opportunity in front of us. We’re building a business that is big, meaningful, and lasting. And we are helping sellers around the world do the same.&amp;lt;br&amp;gt;&amp;lt;br&amp;gt;&amp;lt;strong&amp;gt;&amp;lt;u&amp;gt;Job Description&amp;lt;br&amp;gt;&amp;lt;br&amp;gt;&amp;lt;u&amp;gt;&amp;lt;strong&amp;gt;Our software engineers keep Square simple and make our users faster and smarter by giving them a designed payments experience and rich data surrounding each transaction. We&#39;re looking for engineers of all shapes and sizes, who are excited about building outstanding software and solving hard problems. Our challenges span many technologies, from web and mobile applications (iOS, Android) to server-side development (Java, Ruby). As an engineer at Square, you will work on a small team with people across engineering, product, and creative, building reliable, fast, responsive, and beautiful software.&amp;lt;br&amp;gt;&amp;lt;br&amp;gt;&amp;lt;strong&amp;gt;&amp;lt;u&amp;gt;You Will&amp;lt;br&amp;gt;&amp;lt;u&amp;gt;&amp;lt;strong&amp;gt;&amp;lt;ul&amp;gt;&amp;lt;li&amp;gt;Reliability: Ensure Square works right, every time, by using testing, continuous integration, and in-depth code reviews&amp;lt;li&amp;gt;&amp;lt;li&amp;gt;Security: Create interactions and APIs that promote trust, increase security, and make it harder to do the wrong thing&amp;lt;li&amp;gt;&amp;lt;li&amp;gt;Analytics: Collect all the data around every transaction and turn it into tools that help our users&amp;lt;li&amp;gt;&amp;lt;li&amp;gt;Products: Envision entire new products, features, and flows that are inspired, considered, and magical&amp;lt;li&amp;gt;&amp;lt;li&amp;gt;Fraud Prevention: Make quick decisions on millions of dollars which requires diligence and passion for detecting bad actors and preventing loss&amp;lt;br&amp;gt;&amp;lt;li&amp;gt;&amp;lt;ul&amp;gt;&amp;lt;strong&amp;gt;&amp;lt;u&amp;gt;You Have&amp;lt;br&amp;gt;&amp;lt;br&amp;gt;&amp;lt;u&amp;gt;&amp;lt;strong&amp;gt;&amp;lt;strong&amp;gt;Qualifications&amp;lt;br&amp;gt;&amp;lt;strong&amp;gt;&amp;lt;ul&amp;gt;&amp;lt;li&amp;gt;Pursuing degree in Computer Science, Electrical Engineering, Math or related technical field, graduating between December 2023 and May 2025. <script type="application/ld+json">
      {
      "@context": "https://schema.org",
      "@type": "JobPosting", "datePosted": "2019-11-18T12:00:00+07:00", "description": "&lt;p&gt;For 95% of programming jobs, the primary focus is on using abstractions. For instance, using React JS to build a responsive web portal, or hammering out an API in Express or Rocket. They are about taking ways of seeing the world that others have invented, and applying them to the task at hand, with craftsmanship and skill.&lt;p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;p&gt; &lt;p&gt;We value and respect this work, and our jobs involve a fair share of it, but we are looking for engineers who get up in the morning for the other 5%.&lt;p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;p&gt; &lt;p&gt;We want the abstraction creators: the engineers who are more excited about the technology that doesn’t exist yet than the technology that does.&lt;p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;p&gt; &lt;p&gt;We want people who are dreaming about creating new programming languages or operating system kernels, or even just small NPM packages with APIs that better reflect the problem space than prior abstractions.&lt;p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;p&gt; &lt;p&gt;We need this because the business Bubble is in is taking common patterns for constructing software, and capturing those patterns in repeatable technology, so that they become accessible and intuitive via our visual language. We are in the business of figuring out how to let our users express what they want to create as simply and directly as possible, and then solving the hard problems of taking what they express and running it performantly, scalably, and securely in the cloud.&lt;p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;p&gt; &lt;p&gt;Because we are hiring programmers to design and implement a new language, we don&#39;t have any hard requirements about what technologies you need to know coming in, or what professional experiences you need to have on your resume. Familiarity with our stack is helpful:&lt;p&gt; &lt;p&gt;● AWS&lt;br&gt;● Postgres&lt;br&gt;● Redis&lt;br&gt;● Node&lt;br&gt;● Coffee-Script&lt;br&gt;● ES6&lt;p&gt; &lt;p&gt;...but we are open to people learning on the job.&lt;p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;p&gt; &lt;p&gt;What we look for is a passion and gift for understanding and designing abstractions. That generally corresponds with an intense intellectual curiosity, both within technology and outside of technology, and a deep humility about how much there is to learn and how little we actually know.&lt;p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;p&gt; &lt;p&gt;We do think that years of experience writing code is a must, but we are open to people at all places in their careers. We&#39;re willing to hire new college grads who honed their skills on passion projects, as well as people with a decade of industry experience looking for the next challenge. We are currently only looking for people who want to be hands on writing code, but we value leadership experience or aspirations, since we anticipate that as Bubble&#39;s rapid growth continues, we will build out a world-class engineering team and will need people willing to take on leadership responsibilities as well as people who want to specialize as deep technical experts.&lt;p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;p&gt; &lt;p&gt;In addition to creating better abstractions, the other pole of Bubble&#39;s business is helping our users solve their problems. Our users build everything from personal side projects to VC-backed startups. We are often a critical part of our customers’ operations. As a Bubble engineer, you get a direct feedback loop with customers: our community is incredibly vocal, and whenever we announce a release on our community forum, it always sparks feedback and engagement, and often celebration.&lt;p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;p&gt; &lt;p&gt;So, the other thing we look for and value in our hiring process is people who love to ship code and see it impact people&#39;s lives. We live in a dynamic tension between passionate love for technology in its pure form, and pragmatic caring for the end product. We are backed by &lt;span&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https:medium.comlightspeed-venture-partnerswintermute-makes-sure-you-dont-get-ripped-off-when-you-buy-crypto-63aa96dcb983&quot; style=&quot;font-size: 11pt&quot; class=&quot;postings-link&quot;&gt;Lightspeed&lt;a&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 11pt&quot;&gt;, &lt;span&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https:panteracapital.com&quot; style=&quot;font-size: 11pt&quot; class=&quot;postings-link&quot;&gt;Pantera Capital&lt;a&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 11pt&quot;&gt;, &lt;span&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https:www.sinoglobalcapital.com&quot; style=&quot;font-size: 11pt&quot; class=&quot;postings-link&quot;&gt;Sino Global Capital&lt;a&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 11pt&quot;&gt;, &lt;span&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;http:blockchain.com&quot; style=&quot;font-size: 11pt&quot; class=&quot;postings-link&quot;&gt;Blockchain.com&lt;a&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 11pt&quot;&gt; Ventures, Avon Ventures by &lt;span&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https:www.fidelity.com&quot; style=&quot;font-size: 11pt&quot; class=&quot;postings-link&quot;&gt;Fidelity Investments&lt;a&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 11pt&quot;&gt;, &lt;span&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https:defialliance.co&quot; style=&quot;font-size: 11pt&quot; class=&quot;postings-link&quot;&gt;DeFi Alliance&lt;a&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 11pt&quot;&gt; and other top tier investors. We are run as a technology company, not a financial service provider, and we build our culture around &lt;span&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https:www.wintermute.comjoin-us&quot; style=&quot;font-size: 11pt&quot; class=&quot;postings-link&quot;&gt;core values&lt;a&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 11pt&quot;&gt; of ambition, collaboration, entrepreneurship, transparency and meritocracy.&lt;span&gt; &lt;div&gt; &lt;div&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;div&gt; &lt;div&gt;&lt;b style=&quot;font-size: 18px&quot;&gt;Working at Wintermute DeFi team &lt;b&gt;&lt;div&gt; &lt;div&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 10.5pt&quot;&gt; &lt;span&gt;&lt;div&gt; &lt;div&gt;We are looking for a GraduateJunior Software Developer in DeFi with strong fundamental background in coding and curiosity about DeFi, HFT, market making and crypto trading. At Wintermute, you will be responsible for integrating new protocols right from the start. You will have the opportunity to get a deeper understanding of how various DEX’s trade and be responsible for optimising the execution on those venues, whilst also getting advice and guidance from very experienced developers and traders, including the foundersmanagement team. You will get a lot of independence and responsibility right away, and you&#39;ll learn at an unprecedented speed! No legacy systems, no corporate bureaucracy, no multiple levels of approvals. It is up to you to make an impact. You will act like an owner and your incentives will be completely aligned with those of the company!&lt;div&gt; &lt;div&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 18px&quot;&gt; &lt;span&gt;&lt;div&gt; &lt;div&gt;&lt;b style=&quot;font-size: 18px&quot;&gt;What you will work on &lt;b&gt;&lt;div&gt; &lt;div&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 10.5pt&quot;&gt; &lt;span&gt;&lt;div&gt; &lt;div&gt;A great advantage of this position is that it is varied, and it is also up to you to shape it in the direction that matches your talents and company needs. You will have the opportunity to help integrate DEX’s on chains; includes but not limited to: 1) Improving trading signals for various protocols 2) Improving execution logic to maximise PnL 3) Troubleshooting tradesfailed execution to get a deep understanding of the protocol and improve the trading setup.&lt;div&gt; &lt;div&gt; &lt;div class=&quot;section page-centered&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt; &lt;h3&gt;Hard Skills requirements &lt;h3&gt; &lt;ul class=&quot;posting-requirements plain-list&quot;&gt;&lt;ul&gt; &lt;li&gt;Familiar with at least two of the following programming languages (in Python, Rust, Java, C++) &lt;li&gt; &lt;li&gt;Curiosity in the DeFi space proven by doing extra-curricular projectworkresearch in this space (CeFi trading does not count!)&lt;li&gt; &lt;li&gt;Excellent quantitative and analytical skills &lt;li&gt; &lt;li&gt;Understanding concepts of asynchronous IO &lt;li&gt; &lt;li&gt;Familiarity with Linuxgit &lt;li&gt; &lt;li&gt;Trading knowledge isn’t required but willingness and curiosity to learn algorithmic, high-frequency, quantitative, market making trading and blockchain fundamentals is crucial&lt;li&gt; &lt;ul&gt;&lt;ul&gt; &lt;div&gt;&lt;div&gt; &lt;div class=&quot;section page-centered&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt; &lt;h3&gt;Wintermute Offer &lt;h3&gt; &lt;ul class=&quot;posting-requirements plain-list&quot;&gt;&lt;ul&gt; &lt;li&gt;A unique opportunity to work on very interesting projects, get the level of responsibility and ownership that would be unlikely at any other project or DeFi trading firm&lt;li&gt; &lt;li&gt;A unique opportunity to join one of the strongest and most successful DeFi teams globally&lt;li&gt; we are unable to accept remote candidates&lt;li&gt; &lt;li&gt;Aligned incentive structure: on top of competitive pay, a significant part of your compensation is performance-based variable pay with unlimited upside&lt;li&gt; &lt;li&gt;We offer standard perks too, like pension, private health insurance, free food, but that’s probably not the right reason to join us&lt;li&gt; &lt;ul&gt;&lt;ul&gt; &lt;div&gt;&lt;div&gt; &lt;div class=&quot;section page-centered&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt; &lt;li&gt;Love building things&lt;li&gt; &lt;li&gt;Are curious about algorithmic trading and financial markets&lt;li&gt; &lt;li&gt;Are determined, ambitious yet humble, willing to work hard and learn on the way&lt;li&gt; <h2 style="font-size: 20px;" class="fw-bold ft-5 text-grey">
Software Engineer Intern Crypto Staking Platm
</h2>
</a>
</div>
<div>
<a style="color: white;  font-size: 12px" alt="open" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" href="https://web3.career/software-engineer-intern-crypto-staking-platform-sentry/40377" class="">
<div class="d-flex align-items-center gap-1 gap-md-2">
<div class="myicon " style="background: white; -webkit-mask-image: url(/icons/open.svg); height: 12px; width: 12px"></div>

</a>
</div>
</div>
<div class="mt-2">
<div>
<a style="text-decoration: none; font-size: 12px; color: white" href="/web3-companies/sentry">
Sentry
</a>
<div class="d-flex justify-content-between gap-3 align-items-center">
<div class="text-start">
<div style="font-size: 12px; color: grey;" data-bs-toggle="tooltip" data-bs-placement="top" title="Estimated compensation based on similar jobs">
$70k - $100k<span style="font-family: sans-serif !important;">*</span>
</div>
</div>
<div style="font-size: 12px; color: #d5d3d3;"> CA San Francisco County US</div>
<div class="text-start my-1 d-md-flex justify-content-start gap-3 d-none">
<a class="btn text-center" aria-label="Save this job to favourite" data-turbo-frame="_top" href="/users/sign_up">
<div class="myicon " style="background: #e6007a; -webkit-mask-image: url(/icons/heart.svg); height: 20px; width: 20px"></div>

<a rel="nofollow noopener" href="/i/=czNzADN" target="_blank" class="my-btn my-btn-primary-maximum">

<div style="word-wrap: break-word; word-wrap: break-word; overflow-y: auto; height: calc(100vh - 175px);" class="text-dark-grey-text px-3 pt-2">
<p><strong><u>About This Role<br><br></u></strong>As our Software Engineer Intern, you will have the opportunity to learn about a wide range of technologies at the company, including blockchain protocols, smart contracts, node.js-based backend systems, and react/js-based frontend apps. You will work closely with a group of talented Product Managers, UX Designers, and other Backend/Frontend Engineers. Let us know your interest and passion, and we may even be able to tailor-make an internship specific to you!<br><br><strong>What will you do?<br><br></strong><strong><u>Some Possible Responsibilities Depending On Our Passion And Skillset<br></u></strong></p><ul>
<li style="color:#b3b3b3;">Build new backend services using node.js and Typescript</li>
<li style="color:#b3b3b3;">Develop smart contracts and services that interact with the smart contracts</li>
<li style="color:#b3b3b3;">Build data ETL pipelines using Python</li>
<li style="color:#b3b3b3;">Build frontend apps that are beautiful, simple, and delightful</li>
</ul> <strong>What excites us about you?<br></strong><ul>
<li style="color:#b3b3b3;">You are currently in a reputable Bachelors or Masters program in the US and graduating this year (2022)</li>
<li style="color:#b3b3b3;">You are passionate about blockchain technology and a decentralized future, and you are familiar with the technologies behind blockchains.</li>
<li style="color:#b3b3b3;">You are familiar with one of the following: Solidity/smart contracts, node.js, or React</li>
<li style="color:#b3b3b3;">Able to work independently and set up an efficient development environment</li>
</ul> <strong>What will be great to have?<br></strong><ul>
<li style="color:#b3b3b3;">You are contributing to the open-source community</li>
<li style="color:#b3b3b3;">You have previous internship experiences</li>
<li style="color:#b3b3b3;">You have experience with smart contracts / Solidity (this is a plus but not required, and we will be happy to bring you up to speed on the job)<br>
</li>
</ul><strong><u>To Hear More About This Role You Can<br></u></strong><ul><li style="color:#b3b3b3;"> email - <a href="/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection" class="__cf_email__" data-cfemail="cba5aea2a78ba8b9b2bbbfa4b9aea8b9bea2bfe5a8a4a6">[email&#160;protected]</a><br>
</li></ul><strong>Cryptorecruit are the worlds leading specialist recruiter for the blockchain/Cryptocurrency industry. We recruit positions from CEO,CTO, Project Manager, Solidity developer, frontend and Backend Blockchain developers to marketing/sales and customer service roles. Please browse our website and at www.cryptorecruit.com to search all our job vacancies.</strong>
